lang=EN-US>40%</SPAN>的股权，能够对乙企业施加重大影响。<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>12 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>12 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>31 
</SPAN>日，该项长期股权投资的账面价值为<SPAN lang=EN-US>4 000 </SPAN>万元。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 </SPAN>年，乙企业由于一项主要经营业务市场条件发生变化，当年亏损<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>6 000 </SPAN>万元。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>假定甲企业在取得该投资时，乙企业各项可辨认资产、负债的公允价值与其账面价值相等，双方所采用的会计政策及会计期间也相同。因此，甲企业当年度应确认的投资损失为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2 400 </SPAN>万元。确认上述投资损失后，长期股权投资的账面价值变为<SPAN lang=EN-US>1600 
</SPAN>万元。不考虑相关税费等其他，因素影响。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>如果乙企业<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 
</SPAN>年的亏损额为<SPAN lang=EN-US>12 000 </SPAN>万元，甲企业按其持股比例确认应分担的损失为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>4 800 </SPAN>万元，但长期股权投资的账面价值仅为<SPAN lang=EN-US>4 000 
</SPAN>万元，如果没有其他实质上构成对被投资单位净投资的长期权益项目，则甲企业应确认的投资损失仅为<SPAN lang=EN-US>4 000 
</SPAN>万元，超额损失在账外进行备查登记；在确认了<SPAN lang=EN-US>4 000 
</SPAN>万元的投资损失，长期股权投资的账面价值减记至零以后，如果甲企业账上仍有应收乙企业的长期应收款<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 600 
</SPAN>万元，该款项从目前情况看，没有明确的清偿计划，且在可预见的未来期间不准备收回（并非产生于商品购销等日常活动），则甲企业应进行以下会计处理：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：投资收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 40 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：长期股权投资——损益调整<SPAN lang=EN-US> 40 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：投资收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 8 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：长期应收款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 8 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">6. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">被投资单位除净损益、其他综合收益以及利润分配以外的所有者权益的其他变动被投资单位除净损益、其他综合收益以及利润分配以外的所有者权益的其他变动的因素，主要包括被投资单位接受其他股东的资本性投入、被投资单位发行可分离交易的可转债中包含的权益成分、以权益结算的股份支付、其他股东对被投资单位增资导致投资方持股比例变动等。投资方应按所持股权比例计算应享有的份额，调整长期股权投资的账面价值，同时计入资本公积（其他资本公积），并在备查簿中予以登记，投资方在后续处置股权投资但对剩余股权仍采用权益法核算时，应按处置比例将这部分资本公积转入当期投资收益：对剩余股权终止权益法核算时，将这部分资本公积全部转入当期投资收益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>【例<SPAN lang=EN-US>18</SPAN>】<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>10 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>3 </SPAN>月<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>20 </SPAN>日，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A</SPAN>、<SPAN lang=EN-US>B</SPAN>、<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>C </SPAN>公司分别以现金<SPAN lang=EN-US>200 </SPAN>万元、<SPAN lang=EN-US>400 
</SPAN>万元和<SPAN lang=EN-US>400 </SPAN>万元出资设立<SPAN lang=EN-US>D 
</SPAN>公司，分别持有<SPAN lang=EN-US>D </SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>20%</SPAN>、<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>40%</SPAN>、<SPAN lang=EN-US>40%</SPAN>的政权。<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司对<SPAN lang=EN-US>D </SPAN>公司具有重大影响，采用权益法对有关长期股权投资进行核算。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>D </SPAN>公司自设立日起至<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>12 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>日实现净损益<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1000 </SPAN>万元，除此以外，无其他影响净资产的事项。<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>12 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 
</SPAN>日，经<SPAN lang=EN-US>A</SPAN>、<SPAN lang=EN-US>B</SPAN>、<SPAN lang=EN-US>C 
</SPAN>公司协商，<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司对<SPAN lang=EN-US>D </SPAN>公司增资<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>800 </SPAN>万元，增资后<SPAN lang=EN-US>D </SPAN>公司净资产为<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 
800 </SPAN>万元，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A</SPAN>、<SPAN lang=EN-US>B</SPAN>、<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>C </SPAN>公司分别持有<SPAN lang=EN-US>D </SPAN>公司<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>15%</SPAN>、<SPAN lang=EN-US>50%</SPAN>、<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>35%</SPAN>的股权。相关手续于当日完成。假定<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司与<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>D </SPAN>公司适用的会计政策、会计期间相同，双方在当期及以前期间未发其他内部交易。不考虑相关税费等其他因素影响。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>本例中，<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>12 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>日，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司增资前，<SPAN lang=EN-US>D </SPAN>公司的净资产账面价值为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2 000 </SPAN>万元，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司应享有<SPAN lang=EN-US>D 
</SPAN>公司权益的份额为<SPAN lang=EN-US>400 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 
000</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>20%</SPAN>）。<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司单方面增资后，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>D </SPAN>公司的净资产增加<SPAN lang=EN-US>800 </SPAN>万元，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司应享有<SPAN lang=EN-US>D </SPAN>公司权益的份额为<SPAN lang=EN-US>420 
</SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 800</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>15%</SPAN>）。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司享有的权益变动<SPAN lang=EN-US>20 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>420-400</SPAN>），属于<SPAN lang=EN-US>D 
</SPAN>公司除净损益、其他综合收益和利润分配以外所有者权益的其他变动。<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司对<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>D </SPAN>公司的长期股权投资的账面价值应调增<SPAN lang=EN-US>20 
</SPAN>万元，并相应调整“资本公积——其他资本公积”。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">7. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">投资方持股比例增加但仍采用权益法核算的处理<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>投资方因增加投资等原因对被投资单位的持股比例增加，但被投资单位仍然是投资方的联营企业或合营企业时，投资方应当按照新的持股比例对股权投资继续采用权益法进行核算。在新增投资日，如果新增投资成本大于按新增持股比例计算的被投资单位可辨认净资产于新增投资日的公允价值份额，不调整长期股权投资成本；如果新增投资成本小于按新增持股比例计算的被投资单位可辨认净资产于新增投资日的公允价值份额，应按该差额，调整长期股权投资成本和营业外收入。进行上述调整时，应当综合考虑与原持有投资和追加投资相关的商誉或计入损益的金额。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>【例<SPAN lang=EN-US>19</SPAN>】<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>10 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>日，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司以现金<SPAN lang=EN-US>2500 
</SPAN>万元向非关联方购买<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>20%</SPAN>的股权，并对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司具有重大影响。当日，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司可辨认净资产公允价值与账面价值相等，均为<SPAN lang=EN-US>10 000 
</SPAN>万元。<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>10 </SPAN>年<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>日至<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>13</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 
</SPAN>日期间，<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司实现净损益<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 000 
</SPAN>万元，除此以外，无其他引起净资产发生变动的事项。<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>1</SPAN>日，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司以现金<SPAN lang=EN-US>1200 </SPAN>万元向另一非关联方购买<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>10%</SPAN>的股权，仍对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司具有重大影响，相关手续于当日完成。当日，<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司可辨认净资产公允价值为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1.5 </SPAN>亿元。不考虑相关税费等其他因素影响。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>本例中，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司于<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>10 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>日第一次购买<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司股权时，应享有<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司可辨认净资产公允价值份额为<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 000 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>10 000 
</SPAN>万元×<SPAN lang=EN-US>20%</SPAN>），<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司支付对价的公允价值为<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 500 </SPAN>万元，因此<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>10 </SPAN>年<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>日确认对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司的长期股权投资的初始投资成本为<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 500 </SPAN>万元，其中含<SPAN lang=EN-US>500 
</SPAN>万元的内含商誉。<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：长期股权投资——投资成本<SPAN lang=EN-US> 25 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：银行存款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 25 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">A 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">公司<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>日第二次购买<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司股权时，应享有<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司可辨认净资产公允价值份额为<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 500 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>15 000 
</SPAN>万元×<SPAN lang=EN-US>10%</SPAN>），<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司支付对价的公允价值为<SPAN lang=EN-US>1200 </SPAN>万元，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司本应调整第二次投资的长期股权投资成本为<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 500 </SPAN>万元，并将<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>300 </SPAN>万元的负商誉确认<SPAN lang=EN-US>300 </SPAN>万元的营业外收入，然而，由于<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司第一次权益法投资时确认了<SPAN lang=EN-US>500 
</SPAN>万元的内含正商誉，两次商誉综合考虑后的金额为正商誉<SPAN lang=EN-US>200 </SPAN>万元，因此，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 
</SPAN>日确认的对第二次投资的长期股权投资的初始投资成本仍为<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 200 
</SPAN>万元，并在各查簿中记录两次投资各自产生的商誉和第二次投资时综合考虑两次投资产生的商誉后的调整情况。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：长期股权投资<SPAN lang=EN-US> 12 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：银行存款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 12 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>七、长期股权投资核算方法的转换<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（一）公允价值计量转权益法核算<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>原持有的对被投资单位的股权投资（不具有控制、共同控制或重大影响的），按照金融工具确认和计量准则进行会计处理的，因追加投资等原因导致持股比例上升，能够对被投资单位施加共同控制或重大影响的，在转按权益法核算时，投资方应当按照金融工具确认和计量准则确定的原股权投资的公允价值加上为取得新增投资而应支付对价的公允价值，作为改按权益法核算的初始投资成本。原持有的股权投资分类为可供出售金融资产的，其公允价值与账面价值之间的差额，以及原计入其他综合收益的累计公允价值变动应当转入改按权益法核算的当期损益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>然后，比较上述计算所得的初始投资成本，与按照追加投资后全新的持股比例计算确定的应享有被投资单位在追加投资日可辨认净资产公允价值份额之间的差额，前者大于后者的，不调整长期股权投资的账面价值；前者小于后者的，差额应调整长期股权投资的账面价值，并计入当期营业外收入。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>【例<SPAN lang=EN-US>20</SPAN>】<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>12 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 
</SPAN>月，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司以<SPAN lang=EN-US>600 
</SPAN>万元现金自非关联方处取得<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>10%</SPAN>的股权。<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司根据金融工具确认和计量准则将其作为可供出售金融资产。<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 </SPAN>日，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司又以<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 200 </SPAN>万元的现金自另一非关联方处取得<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>12%</SPAN>的股权，相关手续于当日完成。当日，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司可辨认净资产公允价值总额为<SPAN lang=EN-US>8 000 </SPAN>万元，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司的可供出售金融资产的账面价值<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1 000 </SPAN>万元，计入其他综合收益的累计公允价值变动为<SPAN lang=EN-US>400 
</SPAN>万元。取得该部分股权后，按照<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司章程规定，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司能够对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司施加重大影响，对该项股权投资转为采用权益法核算。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>不考虑相关税费等其他因素影响。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>本例中，<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 </SPAN>日，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司原持有<SPAN lang=EN-US>10%</SPAN>股权的公允价值为<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 
000 </SPAN>万元，为取得新增投资而支付对价的公允价值为<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 200 </SPAN>万元，因此<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>22%</SPAN>股权的初始投资成本为<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 200 </SPAN>万元。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">A 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">公司对<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司新持股比例为<SPAN lang=EN-US>22%</SPAN>，应享有<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司可辨认净资产公允价值的份额为<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 760 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>8 000 
</SPAN>万元×<SPAN lang=EN-US>22%</SPAN>）。由于初始投资成本（<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 200 
</SPAN>万元）大于应享有<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司可辨认净资产公允价值的份额（<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 760 
</SPAN>万元），因此，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司无需调整长期股权投资的成本。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">×<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>13 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 
</SPAN>日，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司确认对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司的长期股权投资，进行会计处理如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：长期股权投资——投资成本<SPAN lang=EN-US> 22 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>资本公积——其他资本公积<SPAN lang=EN-US> 4 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：可供出售金融资产<SPAN lang=EN-US> 10 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>银行存款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 12 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>投资收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 4 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（二）公允价值计量或权益法核算转成本法核算<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>投资方原持有的对被投资单位不具有控制、共同控制或重大影响的按照金融工具确认和计量准则进行会计处理的权益性投资，或者原持有对联营企业、合营企业的长期股权投资，因追加投资等原因，能够对被投资单位实施控制的，应按本指南有关企业合并形成的长期股权投资的指引进行会计处理。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（三）权益法核算转公允价值计量<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>原持有的对被投资单位具有共同控制或重大影响的长期股权投资，因部分处置等原因导致持股比例下降，不能再对被投资单位实施共同控制或重大影响的，应改按金融工具确认和计量准则对剩余股权投资进行会计处理，其在丧失共同控制或重大影响之目的公允价值与账面价值之间的差额计入当期损益。原采用权益法核算的相关其他综合收益应当在终止采用权益法核算时，采用与被投资单位直接处置相关资产或负债相同的基础进行会计处理，因被投资方除净损益、其他综合收益和利润分配以外的其他所有者权益变动而确认的所有者权益，应当在终止采用权益法核算时全部转入当期损益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>【例<SPAN lang=EN-US>21</SPAN>】甲公司持有乙公司<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>30%</SPAN>的有表决权股份，能够对乙公司施加重大影响，对该股权投资采用权益法核算。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>12 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>10 
</SPAN>月，甲公司将该项投资中的<SPAN lang=EN-US>50%</SPAN>出售给非关联方，取得价款<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 800 
</SPAN>万元。相关手续于当日完成。<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>甲公司无法再对乙公司施加重大影响，将剩余股权投资转为可供出售企融资产。出售时，该项长期股权投资的账面价值为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>3 200 </SPAN>万元，其中投资成本<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 600 </SPAN>万元，损益调整为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>300 </SPAN>万元，其他综合收益为<SPAN lang=EN-US>200 
</SPAN>万元（性质为被投资单位的可供出售金融资产的累计公允价值变动），除净损益、其他综合收益和利润分配外的其他所有者权益变动为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>100 </SPAN>万元。剩余股权的公允价值为<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 800 
</SPAN>万元。不考虑相关税费等其他因素影响。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>甲公司有关会计处理如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">1. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">确认有关股权投资的处置损益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：银行存款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 18 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：长期股权投资<SPAN lang=EN-US> 16 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>投资收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">2. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">由于终止采用权益法核算，将原、确认的相关其他综合收益全部转入当期损益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：其他综合收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：投资收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">3. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">由于终止采用权益法核算，将原计入资本公积的其他所有者权益变动全部转入当期损益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：资本公积——其他资本公积<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：投资收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">4. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">剩余股权投资转为可供出售金融资产，当天公允价值为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1 800 </SPAN>万元，账面价值为<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 600 
</SPAN>万元，两者差异应计入当期投资收益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：可供出售金融资产<SPAN lang=EN-US> 18 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：长期股权投资<SPAN lang=EN-US> 16 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>投资收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（四）成本法转权益法<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>因处置投资等原因导致对被投资单位由能够实施控制转为具有重大影响或者与其他投资方一起实施共同控制的，首先应按处置投资的比例结转应终止确认的长期股权投资成本。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>然后，比较剩余长期股权投资的成本与按照剩余持股比例计算原投资时应享有被投资单位可辨认净资产公允价值的份额，前者大于后者的，属于投资作价中体现的商誉部分，不调整长期股权投资的账面价值；前者小于后者的，在调整长期股权投资成本的同时，调整留存收益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>对于原取得投资时至处置投资时（转为权益法核算）之间被投资单位实现净损益中投资方应享有的份额，一方面应当调整长期股权投资的账面价值，同时，对于原取得投资时至处置投资当期期初被投资单位实现的净损益（扣除已宣告发放的现金股利和利润）中应享有的份额，调整留存收益，对于处置投资当期期初至处置投资之日被投资单位实现的净损益中享有的份额，调整当期损益；在被投资单位其他综合收益变动中应享有的份额，在调整长期股权投资账面价值的同时，应当计入其他综合收益；除净损益、其他综合收益和利润分配外的其他原因导致被投资单位其他所有者权益变动中应享有的份额，在调整长期股权投资账面价值的同时，应当计入资本公积（其他资本公积）。长期股权投资自成本法转为权益法后，未来期间应当按照长期股权投资准则规定<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>计算确认应享有被投资单位实现的净损益、其他综合收益和所有者权益其他变动的份额。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>【例<SPAN lang=EN-US>22</SPAN>】<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司原持有<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>60%</SPAN>的股权，能够对<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司实施控制。<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>12 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>11 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>6 </SPAN>日<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司的长期股权投资的账面价值为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>60 00 </SPAN>万元，未计提减值准备，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司将其持有的对<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司长期股权投资中的<SPAN lang=EN-US>1/3 </SPAN>出售给非关联方，取得价款<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>3 600 </SPAN>万元，当日被投资单位可辨认净资产公允价值总额为<SPAN lang=EN-US>16 000 
</SPAN>万元。相关手续于当日完成，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司不再对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司实施控制，但具有重大影响。<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司原取得<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>60%</SPAN>股权时，<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司可辨认净资产公允价值总额为<SPAN lang=EN-US>9 000 </SPAN>万元（假定公允价值与账面价值相同）。自<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司取得对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司长期股权投资后至部分处置投资前，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司实现净利润<SPAN lang=EN-US>5 000 </SPAN>万元。其中，自<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司取得投资日至<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>12 
</SPAN>年年初实现净利润<SPAN lang=EN-US>4 000 </SPAN>万元。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>假定<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司一直未进行利润分配。除所实现净损益外，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司未发生其他计入资本公积的交易或事项。<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司按净利润的<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>10%</SPAN>提取盈余公积。不考虑相关税费等其他，因素影响。本例中，在出售<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>20%</SPAN>的股权后，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司的持股比例为<SPAN lang=EN-US>40%</SPAN>，对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司施加重大影响。对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司长期股权投资应由成本法改为按照权益法核算。有关会计处理如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">1. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">确认长期股权投资处置损益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：银行存款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 36 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：长期股权投资<SPAN lang=EN-US> 20 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>投资收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 16 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">2. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">调整长期股权投资账面价值。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>剩余长期股权投资的账面价值为<SPAN lang=EN-US>4 000 
</SPAN>万元，与原投资时应享有被投资单位可辨认净资产公允价值份额之间的差额<SPAN lang=EN-US>400 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>4 000-9 000</SPAN>×<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>40%</SPAN>）为商誉，该部分商誉的价值不需要对长期股权投资的成本进行调整。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>处置投资以后按照持股比例计算享有被投资单位自购买日至处置投资日期初之间实现的净损益为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1 600 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>4 000</SPAN>×<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>40%</SPAN>），应调整增加长期股权投资的账面价值，同时调整留存收益；处置期初至处置日之间实现的净损益<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>400 </SPAN>万元，应调整增加长期股权投资的账面价值，同时计入当期投资收益。企业应进行以下会计处理：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：长期政权投资<SPAN lang=EN-US> 20 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：盈余公积<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 600 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>利润分配——未分配利润<SPAN lang=EN-US> 14 400 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>投资收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 4 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（五）成本法核算转公允价值计量<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>原持有的对被投资单位具有控制的长期股权投资，因部分处置等原因导致持股比例下降，不能再对被投资单位实施控制、共同控制或重大影响的，应改按金融工具确认和计量准则进行会计处理，在丧失控制之日的公允价值与账面价值之间的差额计入当期投资收益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>【例<SPAN lang=EN-US>23</SPAN>】甲公司持有乙公司<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>60%</SPAN>的有表决权股份，能够对乙公司实施控制，对该股权投资采用成本法核算。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">×<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>12 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>10 </SPAN>月，甲公司将该项投资中的<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>80%</SPAN>出售给非关联方，取得价款<SPAN lang=EN-US>8 000 
</SPAN>万元。相关手续于当日完成。甲公司无法再对乙公司实施控制，也不能施加共同控制或重大影响，将剩余股权投资转为可供出售金融资产。出售时，该项长期股权投资的账面价值为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>8 000 </SPAN>万元，剩余股权投资的公允价值为<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 000 
</SPAN>万元。不考虑相关税费等其他因素影响。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>甲公司有关会计处理如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">1. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">确认有关股权投资的处置损益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：银行存款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 80 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：长期股权投资<SPAN lang=EN-US> 64 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>投资收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 16 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">2. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">剩余股权投资转为可供出售金融资产，当天公允价值为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2 000 </SPAN>万元，账面价值为<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 600 
</SPAN>万元，两者差异应计入当期投资收益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：可供出售金融资产<SPAN lang=EN-US> 20 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：长期股权投资<SPAN lang=EN-US> 16 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>投资收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 4 000 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>八、关于股票股利的处理<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>被投资单位分派股票股利的，投资方不作会计处理，但应于除权日注明所增加的股数，以反映股份的变化情况。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>九、关于投资性主体转变时的会计处理<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>当企业由非投资性主体转变为投资性主体时，其对自转变日起不再纳入合并财务报表范围的于公司采用公允价值计量且其变动计入当期损益，转变日公允价值和原账面价值的差额计入所有者权益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>当企业由投资性主体转变为非投资性主体时，其对自转变日起开始纳入合并财务报表范围的于公司采用成本法进行后续计量。转变日的公允价值为成本法核算的初始成本。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>十、关于处置和相关所得税影响<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（一）处置<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>企业持有长期股权投资的过程中，由于各方面的考虑，决定将所持有的对被投资单位的股权全部或部分对外出售时，应相应结转与所售股权相对应的长期股权投资的账面价值，一般情况下，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>出售所得价款与处置长期股权投资账面价值之间的差额，应确认为处置损益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>投资方全部处置权益法核算的长期股权投资时，原权益法核算的相关其他综合收益应当在终止采用权益法核算时采用与被投资单位直接处置相关资产或负债相同的基础进行会计处理，因被投资方除净损益、其他综合收益和利润分配以外的其他所有者权益变动而确认的所有者权益，应当在终止采用权益法核算时全部转入当期投资收益。投资方部分处置权益法核算的长期股权投资，剩余股权仍采用权益法核算的，原权益法核算的相关其他综合收益应当采用与被投资单位直接处置相关资产或负债相同的基础处理并按比例结转，因被投资方除净损益、其他综合收益和利润分配以外的其他所有者权益变动而确认的所有者权益，应当按比例结转入当期投资收益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>【例<SPAN lang=EN-US>24</SPAN>】<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司持有<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>40%</SPAN>的股权并采用权益法核算。<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>7 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>日，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司将<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>20%</SPAN>的股权出售给第三方<SPAN lang=EN-US>C </SPAN>公司，对剩余<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>20%</SPAN>的股权仍采用权益法核算。<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司取得<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司股权至<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>7 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 
</SPAN>日期间，确认的相关其他综合收益为<SPAN lang=EN-US>400 </SPAN>万元（其中：<SPAN lang=EN-US>350 
</SPAN>万元为按比例享有的<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司可供出售金融资产的公允价值变动，<SPAN lang=EN-US>50 
</SPAN>万元为按比例享有的<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司重新计量设定受益计划净负债或净资产所产生的变动），享有<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司除净损益、其他综合收益和利润分配以外的其他所有者权益变动为<SPAN lang=EN-US>100 
</SPAN>万元。不考虑相关税费等其他因素影响。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">A 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">公司原持有股权相关的其他综合收益和其他所有者权益变动应按如下方法进行会计处理：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">1. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">其他综合收益<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>1</SPAN>）转入当期损益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">350 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">万元的其他综合收益属于被投资单位可供出售金融资产的公允价值变动，由于剩余股权仍继续根据长期股权投资准则采用权益法进行核算，因此，应按处置比例（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>20%/40%</SPAN>）相应结转计入当期投资收益<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>350/2=175</SPAN>（万元）。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>）转入其他的权益科目。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">50 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">万元的其他综合收益属于被投资单位重新计量设定受益计划净负债或净资产所产生的变动，由于剩余股权仍继续根据长期股权投资准则采用权益法进行核算，因此，应按处置比例（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>20%/40%</SPAN>）并按照被投资单位处置相关资产或负债相同的基础进行会计处理。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">2. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">其他所有者权益变动<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>由于剩余股权仍继续根据长期股权投资准则采用权益法进行核算，因此应按处置比例（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>20%/40%</SPAN>）相应结转计入当期投资收益<SPAN lang=EN-US>100/2=50</SPAN>（万元）。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>再假设，<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>12 </SPAN>月，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司再向第三方公司处置<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>15%</SPAN>的政权，剩余<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>5%</SPAN>股权作为可供出售金融资产，按金融资产确认和计量准则进行会计处理。<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司原持有股权相关的其他综合收益和其他所有者权益变动应按以下方法进行会计处理：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">1. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">其他综合收益<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>1</SPAN>）转入当期损益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>处置后的剩余股权改按金融资产确认和计量准则进行会计处理．其他结合收益<SPAN lang=EN-US>175 
</SPAN>万元属于被投资单位可供出售金融资产的公允价值变动，应在转换日全部结转，同时计入当期投资收益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>）转入其他的权益科目。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>处置后的剩余股权改按金融资产确认和计量准则进行会计处理，其他综合收益<SPAN lang=EN-US>25 
</SPAN>万元属于被投资单位重新计量设定受益计划净负债或净资产所产生的变动，按照被投资单位处置相关资产或负债相同的基础进行会计处理。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">2. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">其他所有者权益变动<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>由于剩余股权改按金融资产确认和计量准则进行会计处理，因此，应在转换日全部结转，计入当期投资收益<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>50 </SPAN>万元。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>企业部分处置持有的长期股权投资仍持有剩余股权时，在转换日的会计处理应参看本指南关于长期股权投资核算方法的转换的内容。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>企业通过多次交易分步处置对子公司股权投资直至丧失控制权，如果上述交易属于一揽子交易的，应当将各项交易作为一项处置子公司股权投资并丧失控制权的交易进行会计处理；但是，在丧失控制权之前每一次处置价款与所处置的股权对应得长期股权投资账面价值之间的差额，在个别财务报表中，应当先确认为其他综合收益，到丧失控制权时再一并转入丧失控制权的当期损益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（二）相关所得税影响<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>根据我国《企业所得税法》的相关规定，符合条件的居民企业之间的股息、红利等权益性投资收益为免税收入。因此，通常情况下，当居民企业持有另一居民企业的股权意图为长期持有，通过股息、红利或者其他协同效应获取回报时，其实质所得税率为零，不存在相关所得税费用。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>只有当居民企业通过转让股权获取资本利得收益时，该笔资产转让利得才产生相应的所得税费用。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>从资产负债表角度考虑，资产的账面价值代表的是企业在持续持有及最终处置某项资产的一定期间内，该项资产能够为企业带来的未来经济利益，而其计税基础代表的是在这一期间内，就该项资产按照税法规定可以税前扣除的金额。当资产的账面价值大于其计税基础的，两者之间的差额将会于未来期间产生应税金额，增加未来期间的应纳税所得额及应交所得税，对企业形成经济利益流出的义务。根据《企业会计准则第<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>18 
</SPAN>号——所得税》的相关规定，企业对与子公司、联营企业、合营企业投资等相关的应纳税暂时性差异，应当确认递延所得税负债，只有在同时满足以下两个条件时除外：一是投资企业能够控制暂时性差异转回的时间；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3 
face=宋体>二是该暂时性差异在可预见的未来很可能不会转回。当投资方改变其持有投资意图拟对外出售时，不再符合上述条件，应确认其递延所得税影响。</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P>
<HR>
